The tools spawns’ multiple threads, up to the limit of your CPU, Memory, and Disk Drive performance to unzip as many files simultaneously as possible for maximum performance.\r\nUsing the Tool\r\nThere are now 2 ways to unzip files using this app:\r\n1.\tUnzip all files into the same directories as the zip files.
